or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) (NYSE&#58;FDS) (NASDAQ&#58;FDS), a global provider of integrated financial information, analytical applications, and industry-leading service, today announced results for its fourth quarter ended August&#160;31, 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">Fourth Quarter Fiscal 2020 Highlights</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt;">GAAP revenues increased 5.3%, or $19.3 million, to $383.6 million compared with $364.3 million for the same period in fiscal 2019. The organic growth rate, which excludes the effects of acquisitions, dispositions, and foreign currency movements, was 5.3%. The primary contributors to this growth rate were higher sales in FactSet's wealth and analytics workflow solutions. </font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt;">Operating margin decreased to 25.7% compared with 30.6% for the same period last year </font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">primarily due to a non-cash expense from the impairment of an investment in a company</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">. style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;"> compared with 33.9% in the prior year period </font><font technology.</font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Times the same period in fiscal 2019. </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">Adjusted dil</font><font prior year period primarily driven by a lower tax rate and an improvement in operating results. </font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, compared with 15.5% a year ago, primarily due to excess tax benefits associated with stock-based compensation and finalization of the prior year tax return.  </font></div><div style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">ASV at any given point in time represents the forward-looking revenues for the next twelve months from all subscription services currently supplied to clients and excludes professional services fees billed in the last 12 months that are not subscription-based. Professional services are revenues derived from project-based consulting and implementation.</font></div><div style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">ASV plus professional services was $1.56 billion at August&#160;31, 2020. Organic ASV plus professional services was also $1.56 billion at August&#160;31, 2020, up $78.4 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 5.3%. Organic ASV, which excludes the effects of acquisitions, dispositions, and foreign currency movements, plus professional services, increased $41.3 million over the last three months. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">Buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020 were 5.4% and 4.6%, respectively. Buy-side clients accounted for approximately 84%</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;"> of organic ASV while the remainder is derived from sell-side firms that perform mergers and acquisitions advisory work, capital markets services, and equity research. Americas revenues for the quarter increased to $234.4 million compared with $222.1 million in the fourth quarter last year. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months, the Americas revenue growth rate was 5.5%.</font></div><div style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">ASV from the EMEA region was $426.0 million, increasing 5.7% over the prior year period of $402.9 million. EMEA revenues were $113.8 million compared with $108.9 million from the fourth quarter of fiscal 2019. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the EMEA region revenue growth rate was 4.6%. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">ASV from the Asia Pacific region was $156.5 million, increasing 7.6% over the prior year period of $145.5 million. Adjusted diluted EPS increased 8.7% to $10.87. 2020 marks the 24</font><sup style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;vertical-align:top;">th</sup><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;"> consecutive year that FactSet has increased its adjusted diluted EPS.</font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt;">Net cash provided by operating activities totaled $505.8 million. F</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;">ree cash flow increased 16.4% to $428.2 million.</font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;margin-bottom:10pt;"><font
